import random
from faker import Faker
from datetime import timedelta, date

# Initialize Faker to generate realistic data
fake = Faker()

# Define a function to generate a realistic medical record
def generate_cirrhosis_record():
    # Generate realistic age between 20 and 70 years old
    age_days = random.randint(7 * 365, 70 * 365)
    
    # Generate a random status from the list ['C', 'CL', 'D']
    status = random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'])
    
    # Generate a random number of days since diagnosis
    ndays = random.randint(30, 365 * 3)
    
    # Generate a random drug type, either 'D-penicillamine' or 'Placebo'
    drug = random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'])
    
    # Generate realistic values for the variables based on the rules
    bilirubin = random.uniform(1.0, 20.0)
    cholesterol = random.uniform(150.0, 350.0)
    albumin = random.uniform(2.5, 4.5)
    copper = random.uniform(20.0, 100.0)
    alk_phos = random.uniform(50.0, 150.0)
    sgot = random.uniform(20.0, 100.0)
    tryglycerides = random.uniform(50.0, 300.0)
    platelets = random.randint(100000, 500000)
    prothrombin = random.uniform(10.0, 20.0)
    
    # Determine if the patient has advanced disease (Stage 3 or 4) based on Bilirubin and Albumin
    if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
        stage = random.choice(['3', '4'])
    else:
        stage = random.choice(['1', '2'])
    
    # Assign other variables randomly
    hepatomegaly = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
    spiders = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
    ascites = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
    edema = random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'])
    
    # Generate a fake ID
    id_ = fake.random_int(min=1000000, max=9999999)
    
    # Generate a fake sex
    sex = random.choice(['F', 'M'])
    
    return [id_, ndays, status, drug, age_days, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema, bilirubin, cholesterol, albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, tryglycerides, platelets, prothrombin, stage]

# Generate a list of 10 records
records = [generate_cirrhosis_record() for _ in range(10)]

# Print each generated record
for record in records:
    print(','.join(map(str, record)))

import random

# Define a function to generate realistic patient records
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generate random values within the specified ranges
        id = str(random.randint(10000, 99999))
        ndays = random.randint(30, 365 * 2)  # Number of follow-up days between 30 and 2 years
        status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]  # Randomly select Censored, Transplant, Death
        drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        age = random.randint(30, 80) * 365  # Age in days between 30 and 80 years old
        sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        ascites = ['N', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        hepatomegaly = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        spiders = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        bilirubin = round(random.uniform(1.0, 10.0), 1) if status != 'D' else None  # Bilirubin only relevant if not death
        cholesterol = round(random.uniform(150, 300), 1)
        albumin = round(random.uniform(2.5, 4.0), 1) if status != 'D' else None  # Albumin only relevant if not death
        copper = round(random.uniform(50, 200), 1)
        alk_phos = round(random.uniform(40, 150), 1)
        sgot = round(random.uniform(30, 200), 1)
        tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(50, 200), 1)
        platelets = round(random.uniform(100, 400) * 1000, 1) if status != 'D' else None  # Platelets only relevant if not death
        prothrombin = round(random.uniform(11, 20), 1)
        stage = random.randint(1, 4)  # Randomly select stage 1-4

        record = [id, ndays, status, drug, age, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema, bilirubin, cholesterol,
                  albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, tryglicerides, platelets, prothrombin, stage]

        # Add record to the list if all fields are populated
        if all(record[i] is not None for i in range(len(record))):
            records.append(record)

    return records

# Generate 50 patient records
cirrhosis_records = generate_cirrhosis_records(50)

# Print generated records
for record in cirrhosis_records:
    print(','.join(map(str, record)))

Explanation:
- **ID**: Unique identifier for each patient.
- **N_Days**: Number of days since diagnosis or treatment start.
- **Status**: Outcome of interest ('C' for censored, 'CL' for liver transplant, 'D' for death).
- **Drug**: Treatment received ('D-penicillamine' or 'Placebo').
- **Age**: Age of the patient in days.
- **Sex**: Gender of the patient ('F' for female, 'M' for male).
- **Ascites**: Presence of ascites ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
- **Hepatomegaly**: Evidence of enlarged liver ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
- **Spiders**: Presence of spider naevi ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
- **Edema**: Severity of edema ('N' for none, 'S' for slight, 'Y' for marked).
- **Bilirubin**: Serum bilirubin level (mg/dL), indicating liver function.
- **Cholesterol**: Serum cholesterol level (mg/dL).
- **Albumin**: Serum albumin level (g/dL), a measure of protein levels.
- **Copper**: Serum copper level (µg/dL).
- **Alk_Phos**: Alkaline phosphatase activity (U/L).
- **SGOT**: Aspartate aminotrans

Please generate records in this exact format:
ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin, Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage
import random

# Function to generate random integers within specified ranges
def random_int(min_val, max_val):
    return random.randint(min_val, max_val)

# Function to generate random floats within specified ranges
def random_float(min_val, max_val):
    return round(random.uniform(min_val, max_val), 2)

# Generate patient records
patients = []

# Generate records for patients with advanced disease (Stages 3 or 4)
for i in range(50):
    id = "P" + str(i + 1)
    ndays = random_int(1, 365)
    status = ["C", "CL", "D"][random.randint(0, 2)]
    drug = ["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    age = random_int(40, 80)
    sex = ["F", "M"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    ascites = ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    hepatomegaly = ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    spiders = ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    edema = ["N", "S", "Y"][random.randint(0, 2)]
    bilirubin = random_float(1.0, 10.0)
    cholesterol = random_int(150, 300)
    albumin = random_float(2.5, 4.0)
    copper = random_int(100, 200)
    alk_phos = random_int(40, 150)
    sgot = random_int(50, 150)
    tryglicerides = random_int(100, 500)
    platelets = random_int(50000, 150000)
    prothrombin = random_int(11, 15)
    stage = ["1", "2", "3", "4"][random.randint(0, 3)]

    # Check if the patient has advanced disease criteria met
    if (bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5) and random.randint(0, 1):
        if status == "D":
            stage = "4"
            if edema == "Y" or edema == "marked":
                edema = "marked"
        elif status == "CL":
            stage = "4"
            if ascites == "Y" or hepatomegaly == "Y" or spiders == "Y":
                ascites = "Y"
            else:
                edema = random.choice(["N", "S"])
        elif status == "C":
            stage = "4"
            if ascites == "Y" or edema == "marked":
                ascites = "Y"
            else:
                edema = random.choice(["N", "S"])

    patients.append([id, ndays, status, drug, age, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema, bilirubin, cholesterol, albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, tryglicerides, platelets, prothrombin, stage])

# Print generated records
for record in patients:
    print(record)

# Define a function to generate a random number within a specific range
def generate_random_value(min_value, max_value):
    return round(random.uniform(min_value, max_value), 1)

    N_Days = random.randint(30, 365)
    Status = ["C", "CL", "D"][random.randint(0, 2)]
    Drug = ["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    Age = random.randint(40, 70)
    Sex = ["F", "M"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    Ascites = ["N", "Y"][random.randint(0, 1)]
    Hepatomegaly = ["N", "Y"][random.randint(0, 1)]

    Cholesterol = generate_random_value(100, 300)
    Albumin = generate_random_value(2.5, 5.5)
    Copper = generate_random_value(0.5, 100.0)
    Alk_Phos = generate_random_value(50, 150)
    SGOT = generate_random_value(10, 200)
    Tryglicerides = generate_random_value(50, 400)
    Platelets = generate_random_value(100, 500)
    Prothrombin = generate_random_value(10, 20)
    Stage = random.choice([1, 2, 3, 4])

    # Check if the patient has advanced disease based on bilirubin and albumin levels
    if Bilirubin > 10.0 or Albumin < 2.5:
        Stage = max(Stage, 3)

    # Check if the patient has ascites or edema which could indicate advanced disease
    if Ascites == "Y" or Edema == "Y":
        Stage = max(Stage, 3)

    # Ensure that low platelets and high SGOT levels often co-occur with advanced disease
    if Platelets < 150 or SGOT > 100:
        Stage = max(Stage, 3)

    print(f"{ID}, {N_Days}, {Status}, {Drug}, {Age}, {Sex}, {Ascites}, {Hepatomegaly}, {Spiders}, {Edema}, {Bilirubin}, {Cholesterol}, {Albumin}, {Copper}, {Alk_Phos}, {SGOT}, {Tryglicerides}, {Platelets}, {Prothrombin}, {Stage}")

import random

# Function to generate realistic patient records
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generating random values within specified ranges
        ID = random.randint(1, 10000)
        N_Days = random.randint(0, 180)
        Status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        Drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        Age = random.randint(20, 80)
        Sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        Ascites = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        Hepatomegaly = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        Spiders = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        Edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        Bilirubin = round(random.uniform(0.5, 10), 2)
        Cholesterol = round(random.uniform(100, 300), 2)
        Albumin = round(random.uniform(2.5, 4.5), 2)
        Copper = round(random.uniform(0.5, 100), 2)
        Alk_Phos = round(random.uniform(50, 300), 2)
        SGOT = round(random.uniform(10, 200), 2)
        Tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(50, 500), 2)
        Platelets = round(random.uniform(50000, 500000), 2) // 1000
        Prothrombin = round(random.uniform(10, 30), 2)
        Stage = str(random.randint(1, 4))

        # Applying rules
        if Bilirubin > 10.0 or Albumin < 2.5:
            Stage = max(Stage, '3')
        if Stage == '4':
            Edema = 'Y'
        if Platelets < 150 or SGOT > 100:
            Stage = max(Stage, '3')

        records.append(f"{ID}, {N_Days}, {Status}, {Drug}, {Age}, {Sex}, {Ascites}, {Hepatomegaly}, {Spiders}, {Edema}, {Bilirubin}, {Cholesterol}, {Albumin}, {Copper}, {Alk_Phos}, {SGOT}, {Tryglicerides}, {Platelets}, {Prothrombin}, {Stage}")

    return records

# Generate 10 realistic patient records
num_records = 10
records = generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records)

for record in records:
    print(record)
    print("\n")

**Explanation of the generated records:**

1. **ID**: Unique identifier for each patient.
2. **N_Days**: The number of days since the patient's initial diagnosis or treatment started.
3. **Status**: Indicates whether the patient is still under observation ('C'), received a liver transplant ('CL'), or passed away ('D').
4. **Drug**: The treatment administered, either 'D-penicillamine' or 'Placebo'.
5. **Age**: Age of the patient in days. Note: Age is often measured in years but given in days for consistency with other variables.
6. **Sex**: Gender of the patient ('F' for female, 'M' for male).
7. **Ascites**: Presence of fluid in the abdominal cavity ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
8. **Hepatomegaly**: Enlargement of the liver ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
9. **Spiders**: Spider angiomas on the skin ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no), a symptom of liver disease.
10. **Edema**: Severity of edema ('N' for none, 'S' for slight, 'Y' for marked).
11. **Bilirubin**: Serum bilirubin level in mg/dL.
12. **Cholesterol**: Serum cholesterol level in mg/dL.

import random

def generate_cirrhosis_patient_record():
    id = random.randint(10000, 99999)
    ndays = random.randint(30, 365)
    status_options = ['C', 'CL', 'D']
    status = random.choice(status_options)
    
    drug_options = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']
    drug = random.choice(drug_options)
    
    age_min = 30
    age_max = 70
    age = random.randint(age_min, age_max)
    
    sex_options = ['F', 'M']
    sex = random.choice(sex_options)
    
    # Simulating advanced disease criteria
    if status == 'D':
        bilirubin = random.uniform(15.0, 20.0)
        albumin = random.uniform(2.0, 2.5)
    elif status == 'CL':
        bilirubin = random.uniform(10.0, 15.0)
        albumin = random.uniform(2.5, 3.0)
    else:  # status == 'C'
        bilirubin = random.uniform(5.0, 10.0)
        albumin = random.uniform(2.8, 3.5)
    
    platelets_min = 100
    platelets_max = 150
    platelets = random.randint(platelets_min, platelets_max)
    
    sgot_min = 80
    sgot_max = 120
    sgot = random.uniform(sgot_min, sgot_max)
    
    # Simulating low platelets and high SGOT as co-occurrence indicators
    if platelets < 150:
        copper_min = 100
        copper_max = 200
        copper = random.uniform(copper_min, copper_max)
    else:
        copper_min = 50
        copper_max = 100
        copper = random.uniform(copper_min, copper_max)
    
    alk_phos_min = 50
    alk_phos_max = 100
    alk_phos = random.uniform(alk_phos_min, alk_phos_max)
    
    stage_options = [1, 2, 3, 4]
    stage = random.choice(stage_options)
    
    ascites_options = ['Y', 'N']
    ascites = random.choice(ascites_options)
    
    hepatomegaly_options = ['Y', 'N']
    hepatomegaly = random.choice(hepatomegaly_options)
    
    spiders_options = ['Y', 'N']
    spiders = random.choice(spiders_options)
    
    edema_options = ['N', 'S', 'Y']
    edema = random.choice(edema_options)
    
    cholesterol_min = 150
    cholesterol_max = 250
    cholesterol = random.uniform(cholesterol_min, cholesterol_max)
    
    tryglicerides_min = 50
    tryglicerides_max = 200
    tryglicerides = random.uniform(tryglicerides_min, tryglicerides_max)
    
    prothrombin_min = 12
    prothrombin_max = 18
    prothrombin = random.uniform(prothrombin_min, prothrombin_max)
    
    record = f"{id}, {ndays}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {try

ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin, Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage
import random

def generate_cirrhosis_record():
    id = ''.join([random.choice('0123456789') for _ in range(8)])
    ndays = random.randint(30, 365)
    status_options = ['C', 'CL', 'D']
    drug_options = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']
    age_options = [random.randint(30, 70), random.randint(30, 70)]
    sex_options = ['F', 'M']
    ascites_options = ['Y', 'N']
    hepatomegaly_options = ['Y', 'N']
    spiders_options = ['Y', 'N']
    edema_options = ['N', 'S', 'Y']
    bilirubin_options = random.uniform(0.5, 10)
    cholesterol_options = random.uniform(100, 300)
    albumin_options = random.uniform(2.5, 4)
    copper_options = random.uniform(100, 1000)
    alk_phos_options = random.uniform(50, 200)
    sgot_options = random.uniform(20, 200)
    tryglicerides_options = random.uniform(50, 500)
    platelets_options = random.randint(50, 300)
    prothrombin_options = random.uniform(10, 20)

    stage = None
    if bilirubin_options > 10 or albumin_options < 2.5:
        stage = random.randint(3, 4)
        if stage == 4:
            ascites = 'Y'
            edema = random.choice(edema_options)
    else:
        stage = random.randint(1, 3)

    record = [
        id,
        ndays,
        random.choice(status_options),
        random.choice(drug_options),
        random.choice(age_options),
        random.choice(sex_options),
        random.choice(ascites_options),
        random.choice(hepatomegaly_options),
        random.choice(spiders_options),
        random.choice(edema_options),
        round(bilirubin_options, 2),
        round(cholesterol_options, 2),
        round(albumin_options, 2),
        round(copper_options, 2),
        round(alk_phos_options, 2),
        round(sgot_options, 2),
        round(tryglicerides_options, 2),
        round(platelets_options, 2),
        round(prothrombin_options, 2),
        stage
    ]
    
    return ','.join(map(str, record))

# Generate 10 patient records
for _ in range(10):
    print(generate_cirrhosis_record())

import random

# Function to generate realistic patient records
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generating realistic values based on the given rules
        id_num = random.randint(10000, 99999)
        ndays = random.randint(30, 365 * 5)  # 5 years of follow-up
        status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]  # Randomly choose Censored, Transplant, Death
        drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        age = random.randint(30, 80) * 365  # Age in days
        sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        ascites = ['N', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        hepatomegaly = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        spiders = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        bilirubin = random.uniform(0.5, 15.0)  # Typical range
        cholesterol = random.uniform(100, 400)  # Typical range
        albumin = random.uniform(2.5, 5.0)  # Typical range
        copper = random.uniform(10, 100)  # Typical range
        alk_phos = random.uniform(40, 150)  # Typical range
        sgot = random.uniform(10, 500)  # Typical range
        tryglycerides = random.uniform(50, 400)  # Typical range
        platelets = random.uniform(50000, 600000) / 1000  # Platelet count in ×1000/mm³ typical range
        prothrombin = random.uniform(10, 25)  # Typical range
        stage = ['1', '2', '3', '4'][random.randint(0, 3)]  # Histologic stage
        
        # Check if patient has advanced disease or specific symptoms
        if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
            stage = '3'
        if stage == '4':
            edema = 'Y'
        
        record = f"{id_num}, {ndays}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {tryglycerides}, {platelets}, {prothrombin}, {stage}"
        records.append(record)
    
    return records

# Generate 50 records
num_records = 50
cirrhosis_records = generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records)

for record in cirrhosis_records:
    print(record)
    print("\n")

import random

# Function to generate realistic patient records for liver cirrhosis research
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generate random data within specified constraints
        id = str(random.randint(10000, 99999))
        ndays = random.randint(0, 180)
        status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        age = random.randint(20, 80) * 365  # Age in days
        sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        ascites = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        hepatomegaly = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        spiders = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        bilirubin = random.uniform(0.1, 20) if ndays < 30 else random.uniform(10.1, 20)
        cholesterol = random.uniform(100, 600)
        albumin = random.uniform(1.5, 3.5) if ndays > 30 else random.uniform(2.5, 3.5)
        copper = random.uniform(10, 100)
        alk_phos = random.uniform(45, 150)
        sgot = random.uniform(10, 100)
        tryglicerides = random.uniform(50, 400)
        platelets = random.uniform(50000, 250000) if age < 60 else random.uniform(100000, 250000)
        prothrombin = random.uniform(10, 25)
        stage = ['1', '2', '3', '4'][random.randint(0, 3)]
        
        # Check for advanced disease based on Bilirubin and Albumin
        if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
            stage = ['3', '4'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        
        # Check for Ascites or Edema based on stage
        if stage == '4':
            ascites = 'Y'
            if edema == 'N':
                edema = ['S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        
        # Check for low Platelets and high SGOT
        if stage != '4' and (platelets < 150 or sgot > 100):
            stage = ['3', '4'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        
        # Append generated record to the list
        records.append(f"{id}, {ndays}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {tryglicerides}, {platelets}, {prothrombin}, {stage}")
    
    return records

# Generate 100 records
records = generate_cirrhosis_records(100)

# Print the first 5 records
for record in records[:5]:
    print(record)
    print("\n")

```plaintext
3, 365, CL, D-penicillamine, 5500, M, Y, Y, Y, Y, 12.0, 250, 2.1, 180, 100, 150, 250, 150, 150, 3,
4, 210, D, Placebo, 6000, F, N, N, N, N, 13.5, 180, 2.3, 200, 130, 100, 180, 150, 150, 4,
5, 120, D, Placebo, 3600, M, Y, Y, Y, Y, 14.0, 220, 2.4, 220, 140, 110, 220, 200, 150, 4,
```

In each record:
- **ID** is unique for identification.
- **N_Days** indicates the number of days the patient has been observed.
- **Status** denotes whether the patient was censored (still under observation), received a transplant, or died.
- **Drug** specifies the treatment given to the patient, either D-penicillamine or placebo.
- **Age** represents the patient's age in days.
- **Sex** is marked as 'M' for male or 'F' for female.
- **Ascites**, **Hepatomegaly**, **Spiders**, and **Edema** are indicators of symptoms present in the patient.
- **Bilirubin**, **Cholesterol**, **Albumin**, **Copper**, **Alk_Phos**, **SGOT**, **Tryglicerides**, and **Platelets** are laboratory test results.
- **Prothrombin** measures the time it takes for blood to clot.
- **Stage** is the histologic stage of liver cirrhosis, ranging from 1 to 4.

Please note that these data are synthetic and do not reflect actual patient health information.

import random

# Function to generate realistic patient records
def generate_cirrhosis_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generating realistic values within specified ranges
        id = random.randint(10000, 99999)
        ndays = random.randint(1, 365)
        status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        age = random.randint(30, 80) * 365  # Age in days
        sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        ascites = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        hepatomegaly = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        spiders = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        bilirubin = round(random.uniform(0.5, 20), 1) if random.random() < 0.9 else random.uniform(10.0, 100)
        cholesterol = round(random.uniform(100, 300), 1)
        albumin = round(random.uniform(1.5, 4.0), 1) if random.random() < 0.9 else random.uniform(2.5, 4.5)
        copper = round(random.uniform(20, 200), 1)
        alk_phos = random.randint(40, 200) if random.random() < 0.9 else random.randint(100, 500)
        sgot = random.randint(20, 500) if random.random() < 0.9 else random.randint(100, 500)
        tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(50, 500), 1)
        platelets = round(random.uniform(50, 1000) * 1000) if random.random() < 0.9 else random.uniform(150, 500)
        prothrombin = random.randint(10, 25)
        stage = ['1', '2', '3', '4'][random.randint(0, 3)]

        # Checking for advanced disease criteria
        if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
            stage = ['3', '4'][random.randint(0, 1)]

        # Checking for advanced symptoms in Stage 4
        if stage == '4':
            if random.random() < 0.9:
                ascites = 'Y'
            elif random.random() < 0.8:
                edema = ['S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 1)]

        # Checking for low platelets and high SGOT in specific cases
        if stage == '4' or (stage == '3' and random.random() < 0.5):
            if random.random() < 0.9:
                platelets = max(platelets - random.randint(50, 100), 150)
            if random.random() < 0.9:
                sgot = min(sgot + random.randint(50, 100), 500)

        record = [id, ndays, status, drug, age, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema, bilirubin, cholesterol,
                  albumin

import random

def generate_cirrhosis_record():
    id = str(random.randint(10000, 99999))
    ndays = random.randint(1, 365 * 5)  # 5 years
    status_options = ['C', 'CL', 'D']
    drug_options = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo']
    age_options = [random.randint(30, 80)]  # Assuming typical range for cirrhosis
    sex_options = ['F', 'M']
    ascites_options = ['Y', 'N']
    hepatomegaly_options = ['Y', 'N']
    spiders_options = ['Y', 'N']
    edema_options = ['N', 'S', 'Y']
    bilirubin_options = round(random.uniform(1.0, 20.0), 1)

# Define the range of valid values for each feature
valid_values = {
    'N_Days': [0, 365 * 3],  # Valid number of days from diagnosis to last follow-up
    'Status': ['C', 'CL', 'D'],  # Possible statuses: censored, transplant, death
    'Drug': ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'],  # Possible treatments
    'Age': [0, 365 * 70],  # Age range in days, considering maximum life expectancy
    'Sex': ['F', 'M'],  # Possible sexes
    'Ascites': ['Y', 'N'],  # Possible ascites status
    'Hepatomegaly': ['Y', 'N'],  # Possible hepatomegaly status
    'Spiders': ['Y', 'N'],  # Possible spiders status
    'Edema': ['N', 'S', 'Y'],  # Possible edema status
    'Bilirubin': [0, 20],  # Bilirubin range in mg/dL
    'Cholesterol': [0, 600],  # Cholesterol range in mg/dL
    'Albumin': [2.5, 5],  # Albumin range in g/dL
    'Copper': [0, 100],  # Copper range in µg/dL
    'Alk_Phos': [0, 1000],  # Alkaline phosphatase range in U/L
    'SGOT': [0, 100],  # SGOT range in U/L
    'Tryglicerides': [0, 600],  # Tryglicerides range in mg/dL
    'Platelets': [0, 1000],  # Platelets range in ×1000/mm³
    'Prothrombin': [40, 250],  # Prothrombin time range in seconds
    'Stage': [1, 4]  # Histologic stages range
}

# Generate a record
def generate_record():
    record = [
        f'{random.randint(1000, 9999)}',  # ID
        f'{random.randint(valid_values["N_Days"][0], valid_values["N_Days"][1])}',  # N_Days

        random.choice(valid_values['Sex']),  # Sex
        random.choice(valid_values['Ascites']),  # Ascites
        random.choice(valid_values['Hepatomegaly']),  # Hepatomegaly
        random.choice(valid_values['Spiders']),  # Spiders
        random.choice(valid_values['Edema']),  # Edema
        f'{random.uniform(valid_values["Bilirubin"][0], valid_values["Bilirubin"][1])}',  # Bilirubin
        f'{random.uniform(valid_values["Cholesterol"][0], valid_values["Cholesterol"][1])}',  # Cholesterol
        f'{random.uniform(valid_values["Albumin"][0], valid_values["Albumin"][1])}',  # Albumin

import random
import numpy as np

# Function to generate realistic patient records
def generate_patient_records(num_records):
    records = []
    
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generate realistic values based on the rules provided
        
        # ID generation
        id = f"PID{random.randint(1000, 9999)}"
        
        # N_Days generation
        ndays = random.randint(1, 180)
        
        # Status generation
        status = random.choices(["C", "CL", "D"], weights=[0.8, 0.1, 0.1], k=1)[0]
        
        # Drug generation
        drug = random.choice(["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"])
        
        # Age generation (between 0 and 365 days to simulate a year)
        age = random.randint(0, 365)
        
        # Sex generation
        sex = random.choice(["F", "M"])
        
        # Ascites generation (more likely in advanced stages)
        if random.random() < 0.7:
            ascites = "Y"
        else:
            ascites = "N"
        
        # Hepatomegaly generation (less common)
        hepatomegaly = "N"
        
        # Spiders generation (rarely present)
        spiders = "N"
        
        # Edema generation (more common in advanced stages)
        if random.random() < 0.8:
            edema = random.choice(["N", "S"])
        else:
            edema = "Y"
        
        # Bilirubin generation (advanced disease)
        bilirubin = round(random.uniform(1.5, 10), 1)
        
        # Cholesterol generation (normal range)
        cholesterol = round(random.uniform(150, 250), 1)
        
        # Albumin generation (advanced disease)
        albumin = round(random.uniform(1.5, 2.5), 1)
        
        # Copper generation (normal range)
        copper = round(random.uniform(0.5, 2), 1)
        
        # Alk_Phos generation (normal range)
        alk_phos = round(random.uniform(40, 150), 1)
        
        # SGOT generation (advanced disease)
        sgot = round(random.uniform(50, 200), 1)
        
        # Tryglicerides generation (normal range)
        tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(50, 150), 1)
        
        # Platelets generation (advanced disease)
        platelets = round(random.uniform(50, 100), 1)
        
        # Prothrombin generation (normal range)
        prothrombin = round(random.uniform(11, 15), 1)
        
        # Stage generation (based on other factors)
        stage = random.choice([1, 2, 3, 4])
        
        # Compile record
        record = [id, ndays, status, drug, age, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema, bilirubin, cholesterol, albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, tryglicerides, platelets, prothrombin, stage]
        
        records.append(record)
    
    return records

# Generate 100 patient records
patient_records = generate_patient_records(100)

# Print generated records
for record in patient_records:
    print(record)
    print("\n")

import random
from datetime import timedelta
from faker import Faker
import numpy as np

fake = Faker()

def generate_patient_record():
    # Generate patient ID
    id = fake.uuid4().split('-')[0]

    # Generate number of days for follow-up
    ndays = random.randint(30, 365)

    # Generate status (Censored, Transplant, Death)
    status = random.choices(['C', 'CL', 'D'], weights=[85, 10, 5], k=1)[0]

    # Generate drug treatment (D-penicillamine or Placebo)
    drug = random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'])

    # Generate age in days (within biologically plausible range)
    age = random.randint(30, 80) * 365

    # Generate sex
    sex = random.choice(['F', 'M'])

    # Generate ascites status
    ascites = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])

    # Generate hepatomegaly status
    hepatomegaly = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])

    # Generate spiders status
    spiders = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])

    # Generate edema status (no, slight, marked)
    edema = random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'])

    # Generate bilirubin level (reasonable range)
    bilirubin = round(random.uniform(0.5, 15), 2)

    # Generate cholesterol level (reasonable range)
    cholesterol = round(random.uniform(150, 300), 2)

    # Generate albumin level (reasonable range)
    albumin = round(random.uniform(2.5, 4.5), 2)

    # Generate copper level (reasonable range)
    copper = round(random.uniform(20, 200), 2)

    # Generate alkaline phosphatase level (reasonable range)
    alk_phos = round(random.uniform(40, 200), 2)

    # Generate SGOT level (reasonable range)
    sgot = round(random.uniform(10, 100), 2)

    # Generate tryglicerides level (reasonable range)
    tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(50, 200), 2)

    # Generate platelet count (reasonable range)
    platelets = round(random.uniform(50000, 500000), 0)

    # Generate prothrombin time (reasonable range)
    prothrombin = round(random.uniform(12, 20), 2)

    # Generate stage (1-4)
    stage = random.randint(1, 4)

    # Check if patient has advanced disease based on bilirubin and albumin levels
    if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
        stage = max(stage, 3)

    # Check if patient has ascites or edema, which might indicate advanced disease
    if ascites == 'Y' or edema == 'Y':
        stage = max(stage, 3)

    return [id, ndays, status, drug, age, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema, bilirubin, cholesterol, albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, tryglicerides, platelets, prothrombin, stage]

import random

def generate_cirrhosis_patient_record():
    # Generate patient attributes
    id = random.randint(1, 10000)
    ndays = random.randint(0, 365 * 5)  # 5 years follow-up
    status = random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'])
    drug = random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'])
    age = random.randint(20, 80)
    sex = random.choice(['F', 'M'])
    ascites = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
    hepatomegaly = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
    spiders = random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
    edema = random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'])
    bilirubin = round(random.uniform(1.5, 15), 2)
    cholesterol = round(random.uniform(150, 300), 2)
    albumin = round(random.uniform(2.5, 4.5), 2)
    copper = round(random.uniform(20, 200), 2)
    alk_phos = round(random.uniform(40, 150), 2)
    sgot = round(random.uniform(20, 200), 2)
    triglycerides = round(random.uniform(50, 500), 2)
    platelets = round(random.uniform(100, 600), 2)
    prothrombin = round(random.uniform(10, 25), 2)
    stage = random.randint(1, 4)

    if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
        stage = max(stage, 3)
    if stage == 4:
        if random.random() < 0.8:
            edema = 'Y'
        if random.random() < 0.6:
            ascites = 'Y'

    if albumin < 2.5:
        platelets = min(platelets, 150)

    if sgot > 100:
        platelets = max(platelets, 200)

    record = f"{id}, {ndays}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {triglycerides}, {platelets}, {prothrombin}, {stage}"
    return record

# Generate and print 10 patient records
for _ in range(10):
    print(generate_cirrhosis_patient_record())

import random

# Define parameters for generating data
patient_ids = [f"PID{random.randint(1, 1000)}" for _ in range(100)]
n_days = random.choices(range(1, 365), k=len(patient_ids))
status = ['C' if random.random() < 0.9 else 'CL' if random.random() < 0.05 else 'D' for _ in range(len(patient_ids))]
drug = ['D-penicillamine' if random.random() < 0.5 else 'Placebo' for _ in range(len(patient_ids))]
age = random.choices(range(20, 80), weights=[10] * 30 + [50] * 50 + [20] * 10, k=len(patient_ids))  # Age distribution
sex = random.choices(['F', 'M'], weights=[0.5, 0.5], k=len(patient_ids))
ascites = random.choices(['N', 'Y'], k=len(patient_ids))
hepatomegaly = random.choices(['N', 'Y'], k=len(patient_ids))
spiders = random.choices(['N', 'Y'], k=len(patient_ids))
edema = random.choices(['N', 'S', 'Y'], k=len(patient_ids))
bilirubin = random.choices(range(0, 20), k=len(patient_ids))
chol = random.choices(range(100, 400), k=len(patient_ids))
albumin = random.choices(range(2, 5), k=len(patient_ids))
copper = random.choices(range(10, 100), k=len(patient_ids))
alk_phos = random.choices(range(40, 150), k=len(patient_ids))
sgot = random.choices(range(10, 300), k=len(patient_ids))
triglycerides = random.choices(range(50, 400), k=len(patient_ids))
platelets = random.choices(range(50, 500), k=len(patient_ids))
prothrombin = random.choices(range(10, 25), k=len(patient_ids))
stage = random.choices(range(1, 5), k=len(patient_ids))

# Generate the dataset
dataset = [f"{pid},{nd},{st},{drug},{age[i]},{sex[i]},{asc[i]},{hepat[i]},{spiders[i]},{edema[i]},{bilirubin[i]},{chol[i]},{albumin[i]},{copper[i]},{alk_phos[i]},{sgot[i]},{trig[i]},{platelets[i]},{prothromb[i]},{stage[i]}" 
           for i, pid, nd, st, drug, age, sex, asc, hepat, spiders, edema, bilirubin, chol, albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, trig, platelets, prothromb, stage in zip(patient_ids, n_days, status, drug, age, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema, bilirubin, chol, albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, triglycerides, platelets, prothrombin, stage)]

# Print or return the generated dataset
print("\n".join(dataset))

import random

# Function to generate realistic patient records for liver cirrhosis research
def generate_patient_records(num_records):
    records = []
    for _ in range(num_records):
        # Generating random numbers based on constraints
        id = random.randint(10000, 99999)
        ndays = random.randint(0, 365*5)  # Follow-up period of up to 5 years
        status = ["C", "CL", "D"][random.randint(0, 2)]  # Randomly select status: censored, transplant, death
        drug = ["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"][random.randint(0, 1)]
        age = random.randint(20, 80)
        sex = ["F", "M"][random.randint(0, 1)]
        ascites = ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)]
        hepatomegaly = ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)]
        spiders = ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)]
        edema = ["N", "S", "Y"][random.randint(0, 2)]
        bilirubin = round(random.uniform(0.5, 10.0), 1)
        cholesterol = round(random.uniform(100, 600), 1)
        albumin = round(random.uniform(1.5, 3.0), 1)
        copper = round(random.uniform(50, 500), 1)
        alk_phos = round(random.uniform(50, 500), 1)
        sgot = round(random.uniform(0, 200), 1)
        tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(50, 600), 1)
        platelets = round(random.uniform(50, 600), 1)
        prothrombin = round(random.uniform(10, 25), 1)
        
        # Assigning stage based on the rules provided
        if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
            stage = "3"
        else:
            stage = "4" if (platelets < 150 and sgot > 100) else "2"
        
        # Ensuring values fall within medically reasonable ranges
        if stage == "4":
            if edema == "Y":
                records.append(f"{id}, {ndays}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {tryglicerides}, {platelets}, {prothrombin}, {stage}")
            elif edema == "S":
                records.append(f"{id}, {ndays}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {tryglicerides}, {platelets}, {prothrombin}, {stage}")
        else:

Explanation of generated values:

- **ID**: Unique identifier for each patient.
- **N_Days**: Number of days since the start of treatment or observation.
- **Status**: Indicates whether the patient is still being followed up ('C'), received a transplant ('CL'), or passed away ('D').
- **Drug**: The treatment given, either 'D-penicillamine' or 'Placebo'.
- **Age**: Patient's age in days, calculated from birth date.
- **Sex**: Patient's sex ('M' for male, 'F' for female).
- **Ascites**: Indicates the presence of fluid accumulation in the abdominal cavity ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
- **Hepatomegaly**: Indicates an enlarged liver ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
- **Spiders**: Presence of spider angiomas on the skin ('Y' for yes, 'N' for no).
- **Edema**: Level of edema ('N' for no, 'S' for slight, 'Y' for marked).
- **Bilirubin**: Serum bilirubin level in mg/dL.
- **Cholesterol**: Serum cholesterol level in mg/dL.
- **Albumin**: Serum albumin level in g/dL.
- **Copper**: Serum copper level in µg/dL.
- **Alk_Phos**: Alkaline phosphatase activity in U/L.

import random

# Function to generate a random number within a range
def random_number(min_val, max_val):
    return random.uniform(min_val, max_val)

# Function to generate a random value for specific features based on rules
def generate_feature(feature_name, min_val, max_val):
    if feature_name == 'Age':
        return random.randint(30, 70)
    elif feature_name == 'Sex':
        return random.choice(['F', 'M'])
    elif feature_name == 'Ascites' or feature_name == 'Hepatomegaly' or feature_name == 'Spiders':
        return random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
    elif feature_name == 'Edema':
        return random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'])
    elif feature_name == 'Bilirubin':
        return round(random_number(0.6, 20), 2)
    elif feature_name == 'Cholesterol':
        return round(random_number(100, 300), 2)
    elif feature_name == 'Albumin':
        return round(random_number(2.5, 5), 2)
    elif feature_name == 'Copper':
        return round(random_number(0.5, 10), 2)
    elif feature_name == 'Alk_Phos':
        return round(random_number(40, 150), 2)
    elif feature_name == 'SGOT':
        return round(random_number(0, 300), 2)
    elif feature_name == 'Platelets':
        return round(random_number(100, 1000), 2)
    elif feature_name == 'Prothrombin':
        return round(random_number(9, 20), 2)
    else:
        raise ValueError("Invalid feature name")

**Explanation of the generated records:**

- **ID:** Patient identifier.
- **N_Days:** Number of days since the start of treatment or observation.
- **Status:** Outcome status, indicating whether the patient was censored (still under observation), received a transplant, or died.
- **Drug:** The treatment administered to the patient, either D-penicillamine or Placebo.
- **Age:** Patient's age in days, calculated from birth to the current day.
- **Sex:** Gender of the patient, either Female (F) or Male (M).
- **Ascites:** Indicates the presence or absence of ascites, which is fluid accumulation in the abdomen.
- **Hepatomegaly:** Indicates the presence or absence of hepatomegaly, an enlarged liver.
- **Spiders:** Indicates the presence or absence of spider veins, a symptom associated with liver disease.
- **Edema:** Severity of edema, ranging from no edema (N), slight edema (S), to marked edema (Y).
- **Bilirubin:** Blood bilirubin level, a marker of liver function.
- **Cholesterol:** Serum cholesterol level.
- **Albumin:** Serum albumin level, an indicator of protein levels and liver health.
- **Copper:** Serum copper level.
- **Alk_Phos:** Alkaline phosphatase level.
- **SGOT:** Aspartate aminotransferase level.
- **Tryglicerides:** Serum triglyceride level

import random
from faker import Faker

# Initialize Faker to generate realistic data
fake = Faker()

def generate_patient_record():
    # Generate realistic data based on the given medical rules
    id = fake.uuid4()[:8]  # Generate a unique ID
    
    # Days can be any number up to 365 days for simplicity
    ndays = random.randint(1, 365)
    
    # Status can be C (censored), CL (transplant), or D (death)
    status = random.choice(["C", "CL", "D"])
    
    # Drug can be D-penicillamine or Placebo
    drug = random.choice(["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"])
    
    # Age in days, typically a patient would not be younger than 1 day or older than 365 days for simplicity
    age = random.randint(1, 365)
    
    # Sex can be F (female) or M (male)
    sex = random.choice(["F", "M"])
    
    # Ascites can be Y (yes) or N (no)
    ascites = random.choice(["Y", "N"])
    
    # Hepatomegaly can be Y (yes) or N (no)
    hepatomegaly = random.choice(["Y", "N"])
    
    # Spiders can be Y (yes) or N (no)
    spiders = random.choice(["Y", "N"])
    
    # Edema can be N (no), S (slight), or Y (marked)
    edema = random.choice(["N", "S", "Y"])
    
    # Bilirubin level in mg/dL
    bilirubin = round(random.uniform(1.0, 10.0), 1) if status != 'D' else round(random.uniform(10.0, 15.0), 1)
    
    # Cholesterol level in mg/dL
    cholesterol = round(random.uniform(150.0, 300.0), 1)
    
    # Albumin level in g/dL
    albumin = round(random.uniform(2.5, 4.5), 1) if status != 'D' else round(random.uniform(1.5, 2.0), 1)
    
    # Copper level in µg/dL
    copper = round(random.uniform(10.0, 200.0), 1)
    
    # Alkaline phosphatase level in U/L
    alk_phos = round(random.uniform(40.0, 200.0), 1)
    
    # SGOT level in U/L
    sgot = round(random.uniform(10.0, 150.0), 1) if status != 'D' else round(random.uniform(100.0, 300.0), 1)
    
    # Tryglicerides level in mg/dL
    tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(50.0, 200.0), 1)
    
    # Platelets count in ×1000/mm³
    platelets = round(random.uniform(100.0, 500.0), 1)
    
    # Prothrombin time in seconds
    prothrombin = round(random.uniform(12.0, 25.0), 1)
    
    # Stage based on medical rules
    stage = str(random.randint(1, 4)) if status != 'D' else '4'
    
    return f"{id},{ndays},{status},{drug},{age},{sex},{ascites},{hepatomegaly},{spiders},{edema},{

import random
import numpy as np

# Define a function to generate realistic patient records
def generate_cirrhosis_record():
    # Generate random attributes within specified ranges
    id = str(random.randint(1000, 9999))
    ndays = random.randint(30, 180)  # Number of follow-up days
    status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]  # Censored, Transplant, Death
    
    drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    
    age = random.randint(30, 70) * 365  # Age in days
    sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    
    ascites = ['N', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    hepatomegaly = ['N', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    spiders = ['N', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
    
    bilirubin = round(np.random.uniform(0.5, 10), 1) if status != 'D' else np.random.uniform(10.1, 20)
    cholesterol = round(np.random.uniform(100, 300), 1)
    albumin = round(np.random.uniform(2.5, 4), 1)
    copper = round(np.random.uniform(0.1, 100), 1)
    alk_phos = round(np.random.uniform(25, 200), 1)
    sgot = round(np.random.uniform(0, 200), 1)
    tryglicerides = round(np.random.uniform(50, 500), 1)
    platelets = round(np.random.uniform(100, 500), 1)
    prothrombin = round(np.random.uniform(10, 20), 1)
    
    stage = ['1', '2', '3', '4'][random.randint(0, 3)]
    
    # Check conditions based on the generated values
    if (bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5) and status not in ['C', 'D']:
        stage = '3'
    elif (bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5) and (ascites == 'Y' or edema != 'N'):
        stage = '4'
    if (platelets < 150 or sgot > 100) and status not in ['C', 'D']:
        stage = '3'
    
    return f"{id}, {ndays}, {status}, {drug}, {age}, {sex}, {ascites}, {hepatomegaly}, {spiders}, {edema}, {bilirubin}, {cholesterol}, {albumin}, {copper}, {alk_phos}, {sgot}, {tryglicerides}, {platelets}, {prothrombin}, {stage}"

# Generate 10 patient records
patient_records = [generate_cirrhosis_record() for _ in range(10)]

for record in patient_records:
    print(record)

2. Stage 4 patients usually have Ascites=Y or Edema=Y
3. Low Platelets (<150) and high SGOT (>100) often co-occur
4. Drug is either D-penicillamine or Placebo
5. Ensure values fall within medically reasonable ranges

Features:

1. ID: Patient ID  
2. N_Days: Number of follow-up days  
3. Status: C=censored, CL=transplant, D=death  
4. Drug: Treatment type (D-penicillamine or Placebo)  
5. Age: Patient's age in days  
6. Sex: F or M  
7. Ascites: Y or N  
8. Hepatomegaly: Y or N  
9. Spiders: Y or N  
10. Edema: N=no, S=slight, Y=marked  
11. Bilirubin: mg/dL  
12. Cholesterol: mg/dL  
13. Albumin: g/dL  
14. Copper: µg/dL  
15. Alk_Phos: alkaline phosphatase (U/L)  
16. SGOT: aspartate aminotransferase (U/L)  
17. Tryglicerides: mg/dL  
18. Platelets: count (×1000/mm³)  
19. Prothrombin: seconds  
20. Stage: histologic stage (1-4)

Please generate records in this exact format:
ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin, Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage
import random
import numpy as np

def generate_cirrhosis_patient_record():
    # Define reasonable ranges for each variable
    min_age = 20
    max_age = 80
    min_bilirubin = 0.6
    max_bilirubin = 20.0
    min_albumin = 2.5
    max_albumin = 5.5
    min_cholesterol = 100
    max_cholesterol = 500
    min_copper = 10
    max_copper = 1000
    min_alk_phos = 40
    max_alk_phos = 200
    min_sgot = 10
    max_sgot = 100
    min_platelets = 50000
    max_platelets = 500000
    min_prothrombin = 60
    max_prothrombin = 140
    
    # Generate patient records
    records = []
    for _ in range(100):
        id = random.randint(1, 10000)
        ndays = random.randint(1, 1000)
        status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]
        drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        
        age = random.randint(min_age, max_age)
        sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
        
        bilirubin = random.uniform(min_bilirubin, max_bilirubin)
        cholesterol = random.uniform(min_cholesterol, max_cholesterol)
        albumin = random.uniform(min_albumin, max_albumin)
        copper = random.uniform(min_copper, max_copper)
        alk_phos = random.uniform(min_alk_phos, max_alk_phos)
        sgot = random.uniform(min_sgot, max_sgot)
        triglycerides = random.uniform(0.2, 300)
        platelets = random.uniform(min_platelets, max_platelets)
        prothrombin = random.uniform(min_prothrombin, max_prothrombin)
        
        # Check if patient has advanced disease based on bilirubin and albumin levels
        stage = 1
        if bilirubin > 10.0 or albumin < 2.5:
            stage = random.randint(3, 4)
            
            # If in stage 4, randomly assign ascites or edema
            if stage == 4:
                ascites = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
                edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
            else:
                ascites = 'N'
                edema = 'N'
                
        else:
            ascites = 'N'
            edema = 'N'
        
        # Generate records based on the defined rules
        record = [
            id,
            ndays,
            status,
            drug,
            age,
            sex,
            ascites,
            'Y' if stage >= 3 else ('N' if stage == 1 else ''),
            'Y' if stage >= 3 else ('N' if stage == 1 else ''),
            edema,
            bilirubin,
            cholesterol,
            albumin,
            copper,
            alk_phos,
            sgot,
            triglycerides,
            platelets,
            prothrombin,
            stage
        ]
        
        records.append(record)
    
    return records

# Example usage
records = generate_cirrh

1. Patients with higher Bilirubin (>10.0) or lower Albumin (<2.5) often have advanced disease (Stage 3 or 4)
2. Stage 4 patients usually have Ascites=Y or Edema=Y

ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin, Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage
import random

def generate_patient_record():
    id = random.randint(10000, 99999)
    ndays = random.randint(30, 365 * 5)  # 5 years
    status = ['C', 'CL', 'D'][random.randint(0, 2)]
    drug = ['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    age = random.randint(30, 80) * 365  # Age in days
    sex = ['F', 'M'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    ascites = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    hepatomegaly = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    spiders = ['Y', 'N'][random.randint(0, 1)]
    edema = ['N', 'S', 'Y'][random.randint(0, 2)]
    bilirubin = round(random.uniform(1, 10), 1)
    cholesterol = round(random.uniform(150, 300), 1)
    albumin = round(random.uniform(2.5, 5), 1)
    copper = round(random.uniform(50, 300), 1)
    alk_phos = round(random.uniform(40, 200), 1)
    sgot = round(random.uniform(10, 100), 1)
    tryglicerides = round(random.uniform(100, 400), 1)
    platelets = round(random.uniform(100, 600) * 1000)  # in ×1000/mm³
    prothrombin = round(random.uniform(10, 20), 1)
    stage = str(random.randint(1, 4))

    if bilirubin > 10 or albumin < 2.5:
        if bilirubin > 10:
            stage = '3'
        if albumin < 2.5:
            stage = '3' if stage != '4' else stage
        if random.random() < 0.5:
            edema = 'Y'

    if random.random() < 0.3 and stage == '4':
        edema = 'Y'
    elif random.random() < 0.1:
        ascites = 'Y'

    if random.random() < 0.3 and (bilirubin > 10 or albumin < 2.5):
        platelets = round(platelets * random.uniform(0.5, 0.8), 0)
        if platelets < 150:
            stage = '4'

    if random.random() < 0.2 and stage == '4':
        sgot = round(sgot * random.uniform(1.5, 2.5), 1)

    return [id, ndays, status, drug, age, sex, ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, edema,
            bilirubin, cholesterol, albumin, copper, alk_phos, sgot, tryglicerides,
            platelets, prothrombin, stage]

# Generate multiple records
records = [generate_patient_record() for _ in range(10)]

for record in records:
    print(','.join(map(str, record)))

Please note that the generated data is intended to be illustrative and may not reflect real-world patient data exactly due to the synthetic nature of the generation process.

In each record:
- The `ID` identifies the patient.
- `N_Days` represents the number of days since the start of treatment or diagnosis.
- `Status` indicates whether the patient is censored (`C`), has undergone a transplant (`CL`), or has died (`D`).
- `Drug` denotes the treatment received (either `D-penicillamine` or `Placebo`).
- `Age` is given in days, which may seem unusual for medical reports but is included here as requested.
- `Sex` is indicated by `M` for male or `F` for female.
- `Ascites`, `Hepatomegaly`, and `Spiders` are binary indicators of symptoms presence or absence.
- `Edema` indicates the severity level of edema present.
- `Bilirubin`, `Cholesterol`, `Albumin`, `Copper`, `Alk_Phos`, `SGOT`, `Tryglicerides`, `Platelets`, `Prothrombin`, and `Stage` are physiological indicators and disease stage, respectively.

You are a synthetic medical data generator. Please generate realistic cirrhosis patient records following these medical rules:

1. Patients with higher Bilirubin (>10.0) or lower Albumin (<2.5) often have advanced disease (Stage 3 or 4)
2. Stage 4 patients usually have Ascites=Y or Edema=Y
